Zayn and Ingrid have so kindly, gently put what I needed to hear in a beautiful melody. I've been so numb the whole of last year, sitting in a perpetual fear of the world ending, having seen so many deaths around me and yet wanting to hold onto life so tightly. It's so surreal to wake up everyday and walk and talk as if the last year hasn't altered me completely. As if it hasn't taken parts of my soul and crushed and broke them into pieces. I've never before felt so powerless, helpless and empty as if nothing I did mattered. It's so hard to go through life with this feeling sitting in your chest and now that things are finally looking up a little bit (I actually have started seeing children come out of their homes and play owing to the summer break), I do not know how to go back, how to fix myself, I don't know which broken piece fits where.
